(the &#8220;Company&#8221;) (NASDAQ: EBTC), parent of Enterprise Bank, announces net income for the three months ended </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">June&#160;30, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$3.5 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, an increase of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$201 thousand</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">6%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, compared to the same three-month period in </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">.  Diluted earnings per share were </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$0.34</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;for the three months ended </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">June&#160;30, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, an </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">increase</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">6%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;compared to the same three-month period in </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">.  Net income for the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">six</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;months ended </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">June&#160;30, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;amounted to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$7.1 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, an increase of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$315 thousand</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">5%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, compared to the same </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">six</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">-month period in </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">.  Diluted earnings per share were </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$0.69</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;for the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">six</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">-month period ended </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">June&#160;30, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, an </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">increase</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">3%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, compared to same period in </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#160;&#160;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">As previously announced on </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">July&#160;21, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, the Company declared a quarterly dividend of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">$0.125</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;per share to be paid on </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">September&#160;1, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;to shareholders of record as of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">August&#160;11, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">.  The </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;dividend rate represents a </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">4.2%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;increase over the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;dividend rate.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">Chief Executive Officer Jack Clancy commented, &#8220;We have had strong growth in </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, particularly in the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">second</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;quarter.  For the first </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">six</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;months of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, loans have increased </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$64 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">4%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, and deposits, excluding brokered deposits, have increased </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$157 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">9%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">.  Assets, loans and deposits have increased by </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">12%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">9%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, and </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">11%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, respectively, compared to a year ago.  We also continued to show growth in all of our business lines including insurance, cash management, and our wealth management and trust business as we continue to provide competitive solutions to meet our customers&#8217; financial needs.  This growth positions us well as we enter the second half of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">.&#8221;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">Founder and Chairman of the Board George Duncan commented, &#8220;Our growth continues to be driven by the collective efforts and contributions of our dedicated Enterprise team, active community involvement, relationship building and a customer-focused mindset, market expansion, and ongoing enhancement of our state-of-the-art product and service offerings.  Our comprehensive services include commercial lending, cash management, digital banking, wealth management, trust services, and insurance services.  Strategically, our focus remains on organic growth and continually planning for and investing in our future.&#8221;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">Results of Operations</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">The Company&#8217;s </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;growth contributed to increases in quarterly and year-to-date net interest income, non-interest income, and non-interest expenses, as compared to the same periods in </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">.  Quarter and year-to-date net income in </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;was also impacted by increases in net gains on sales of investment securities and the provision for loan losses compared to the same </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;periods.  The current year-to-date period also included one-time expenses related to the redemption, in March 2015, of the Trust Preferred Securities issued in 2000. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">Net interest income for the three months ended </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">June&#160;30, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;amounted to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$19.0 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, an increase of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$1.5 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">9%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, compared to the same period in </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">.  Net interest income for the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">six</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;months ended </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">June&#160;30, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;amounted to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$37.4 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, an increase of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$3.1 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">9%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, compared to the same period in </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">.  The increase in net interest income was due primarily to loan growth, partially offset by a decrease in tax equivalent net interest margin (&#8220;margin&#8221;).  Average loan balances (including loans held for sale) increased </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$137.0 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;and </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$142.7 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;for the three and six months ended </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">June&#160;30, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, respectively, compared to the same </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;period averages.  Net interest margin was </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">3.93%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;for the quarter ended </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">June&#160;30, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, which is down from the quarterly margin of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">4.04%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;for the three months ended </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">June&#160;30, 2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">.  The </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">March&#160;31, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;quarterly margin was </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">3.95%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">.  Margin was </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">3.94%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;for the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">six</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;months ended </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">June&#160;30, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, compared to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">4.03%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;for the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">six</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;months ended </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">June&#160;30, 2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">For the three months ended </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">June&#160;30, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;and </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, the provision for loan losses amounted to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$1.2 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;and </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$200 thousand</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, respectively.  The year-to-date provision for loan losses amounted to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$1.9 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;and </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$400 thousand</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;for </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;and </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, respectively.  The increase in the 2015 provision was primarily due to additional </font></div><br><div style="text-align:center;"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="s57CB2E42D1EB550D83EE356BD3D68312"></a><br><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">specific reserves on impaired commercial loans and commercial loan charge-offs.  In determining the provision for the allowance for loan losses, management takes into consideration the level of loan growth and an estimate of credit risk, which includes such items as adversely classified and non-performing loans, the estimated specific reserves needed for impaired loans, the level of net charge-offs, and the estimated impact of current economic conditions on credit quality.  Loan growth for the six months ended </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">June&#160;30, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;was </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$63.9 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;compared to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$67.3 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;during the six months ended </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">June&#160;30, 2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">.  Total non-performing loans as a percentage of total loans declined to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">0.92%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;at </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">June&#160;30, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, compared to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">1.13%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;at </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">June&#160;30, 2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">.  The balance of the allowance for loan losses allocated to impaired loans amounted to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$2.6 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;at </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">June&#160;30, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, compared to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$2.9 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;at </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">June&#160;30, 2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">.  For the six months ended </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">June&#160;30, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, the Company recorded net charge-offs of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$809 thousand</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;compared to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$839 thousand</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in net charge-offs for the same period ended </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">June&#160;30, 2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">.  The majority of the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;charge-offs were previously allocated specific reserves on commercial relationships which contributed to the lower provision for loan losses in </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">.  The allowance for loan losses to total loans ratio was </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">1.62%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;at both </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">June&#160;30, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;and </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">December&#160;31, 2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, compared to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">1.67%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;at </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">June&#160;30, 2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">Non-interest income for the three months ended </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">June&#160;30, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;amounted to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$3.9 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, an increase of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$628 thousand</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">19%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, compared to the same period in </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">.  Non-interest income for the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">six</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;months ended </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">June&#160;30, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;amounted to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$7.9 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, an increase of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$1.2 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">18%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, compared to the same period in </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">.  The increase in non-interest income was primarily due to increases in net gains on the sales of investment securities and to a lesser extent, increased miscellaneous other income, which was primarily impacted by higher loan prepayment fees.  Year-to-date non-interest income also benefited from increases in investment advisory fee income and gains on loan sales, as well as gains on sales of other real estate owned (OREO), partially offset by the net loss on the Company&#8217;s Capital Trust subsidiary due to the write-off of debt issuance costs related to the redemption of Trust Preferred Securities (Subordinated Debt) in March 2015. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">Non-interest expense for the quarter ended </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">June&#160;30, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;amounted to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$16.3 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, an increase of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$822 thousand</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">5%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, compared to the same period in the prior year.  For the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">six</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;months ended </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">June&#160;30, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, non-interest expense amounted to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$32.5 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, an increase of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$2.2 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">7%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, over the same period in the prior year.  These increases primarily were due to increases in salaries and benefits and occupancy expenses, mainly resulting from the Company&#8217;s strategic growth initiatives, partially offset by a decrease in audit, legal and other professional costs.  Year-to-date non-interest expense was also impacted by higher technology and advertising costs associated with the Company&#8217;s strategic growth initiatives, and higher miscellaneous other expenses primarily due to the prepayment fees associated with the redemption of the Trust Preferred Securities, partially offset by lower investment advisory and custodial expenses. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">Key Financial Highlights</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; The Company is principally engaged in the business of attracting deposits from the general public and investing in commercial loans and investment securities.  Through Enterprise Bank and its subsidiaries, the Company offers a range of commercial and consumer loan products, and deposit and cash management services.  The Company also offers investment advisory and wealth management, trust, and insurance services.  The Company&#8217;s headquarters and the bank's main office are located at 222 Merrimack Street in Lowell, Massachusetts.  The Company&#8217;s primary market area is the greater Merrimack Valley and North Central regions of Massachusetts and Southern New Hampshire.  Enterprise Bank has </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">22</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;full-service branch offices located in the Massachusetts cities and towns of Lowell, Acton, Andover, Billerica, Chelmsford, Dracut, Fitchburg, Lawrence, Leominster, Methuen, Tewksbury, Tyngsborough and Westford and in the New Hampshire towns of Derry, Hudson, Nashua, Pelham and Salem.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">This earnings release contains statements about future events that constitute forward-looking statements within the meaning of the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995.
